[2018/08/24 09:25:45] SQL Query: SELECT t.id_plan,t.nombre,t.promocional,t.duracion,t.extension,t.porc_descarga,t.num_post,t.costo, 
        GROUP_CONCAT(a.accion ORDER BY p.id_permisoPlan) as acciones, GROUP_CONCAT(a.descripcion ORDER BY p.id_permisoPlan) as descripciones
        FROM mfo_permisoplan p
        INNER JOIN mfo_accionsist a ON a.id_accionSist = p.id_accionSist 
        INNER JOIN mfo_plan t ON t.id_plan = p.id_plan 
        WHERE a.estado = 1
        AND t.tipo_plan = 2
        AND t.tipo_usuario = 1
        AND t.id_sucursal = 1
        GROUP BY t.id_plan
        ORDER BY p.id_permisoPlan;
[2018/08/24 09:25:45] SQL Query: SELECT t.id_plan,t.nombre,t.promocional,t.duracion,t.extension,t.porc_descarga,t.num_post,t.costo, 
        GROUP_CONCAT(a.accion ORDER BY p.id_permisoPlan) as acciones, GROUP_CONCAT(a.descripcion ORDER BY p.id_permisoPlan) as descripciones
        FROM mfo_permisoplan p
        INNER JOIN mfo_accionsist a ON a.id_accionSist = p.id_accionSist 
        INNER JOIN mfo_plan t ON t.id_plan = p.id_plan 
        WHERE a.estado = 1
        AND t.tipo_plan = 1
        AND t.tipo_usuario = 1
        AND t.id_sucursal = 1
        GROUP BY t.id_plan
        ORDER BY p.id_permisoPlan;

        FROM mfo_permisoplan p
        INNER JOIN mfo_accionsist a ON a.id_accionSist = p.id_accionSist 
        INNER JOIN mfo_plan t ON t.id_plan = p.id_plan 
        WHERE a.estado = 1
        AND t.tipo_plan = 2

[2018/08/24 09:36:17] SQL Query: SELECT t.id_plan,t.nombre,t.promocional,t.duracion,t.extension,t.porc_descarga,t.num_post,t.costo, 
        GROUP_CONCAT(a.accion ORDER BY p.id_permisoPlan) as acciones, GROUP_CONCAT(a.descripcion ORDER BY p.id_permisoPlan) as descripciones
        FROM mfo_permisoplan p
        INNER JOIN mfo_accionsist a ON a.id_accionSist = p.id_accionSist 
        INNER JOIN mfo_plan t ON t.id_plan = p.id_plan 
        WHERE a.estado = 1
        AND t.tipo_plan = 2
        AND t.tipo_usuario = 2
        AND t.id_sucursal = 1
        GROUP BY t.id_plan
        ORDER BY p.id_permisoPlan;
[2018/08/24 09:36:17] SQL Query: SELECT t.id_plan,t.nombre,t.promocional,t.duracion,t.extension,t.porc_descarga,t.num_post,t.costo, 
        GROUP_CONCAT(a.accion ORDER BY p.id_permisoPlan) as acciones, GROUP_CONCAT(a.descripcion ORDER BY p.id_permisoPlan) as descripciones
        FROM mfo_permisoplan p
        INNER JOIN mfo_accionsist a ON a.id_accionSist = p.id_accionSist 
        INNER JOIN mfo_plan t ON t.id_plan = p.id_plan 
        WHERE a.estado = 1
        AND t.tipo_plan = 1
        AND t.tipo_usuario = 2
        AND t.id_sucursal = 1
        GROUP BY t.id_plan
        ORDER BY p.id_permisoPlan;

        GROUP_CONCAT(a.accion ORDER BY p.id_permisoPlan) as acciones, GROUP_CONCAT(a.descripcion ORDER BY p.id_permisoPlan) as descripciones
        FROM mfo_permisoplan p
        INNER JOIN mfo_accionsist a ON a.id_accionSist = p.id_accionSist 
        INNER JOIN mfo_plan t ON t.id_plan = p.id_plan 
        WHERE a.estado = 1
        AND t.tipo_plan = 2
        AND t.tipo_usuario = 2
        AND t.id_sucursal = 1
        GROUP BY t.id_plan
        ORDER BY p.id_permisoPlan;

        GROUP_CONCAT(a.accion ORDER BY p.id_permisoPlan) as acciones, GROUP_CONCAT(a.descripcion ORDER BY p.id_permisoPlan) as descripciones
        FROM mfo_permisoplan p
        INNER JOIN mfo_accionsist a ON a.id_accionSist = p.id_accionSist 
        INNER JOIN mfo_plan t ON t.id_plan = p.id_plan 
        WHERE a.estado = 1
        AND t.tipo_plan = 1
        AND t.tipo_usuario = 2
        AND t.id_sucursal = 1
        GROUP BY t.id_plan
        ORDER BY p.id_permisoPlan;

[2018/08/24 09:46:25] SQL Query: SELECT t.id_plan,t.nombre,t.promocional,t.duracion,t.extension,t.porc_descarga,t.num_post,t.costo, 
        GROUP_CONCAT(a.accion ORDER BY p.id_permisoPlan) as acciones, GROUP_CONCAT(a.descripcion ORDER BY p.id_permisoPlan) as descripciones
        FROM mfo_permisoplan p
        INNER JOIN mfo_accionsist a ON a.id_accionSist = p.id_accionSist 
        INNER JOIN mfo_plan t ON t.id_plan = p.id_plan 
        WHERE a.estado = 1
        AND t.tipo_plan = 2
        AND t.tipo_usuario = 2
        AND t.id_sucursal = 1
        GROUP BY t.id_plan
        ORDER BY p.id_permisoPlan;
[2018/08/24 09:46:25] SQL Query: SELECT t.id_plan,t.nombre,t.promocional,t.duracion,t.extension,t.porc_descarga,t.num_post,t.costo, 
        GROUP_CONCAT(a.accion ORDER BY p.id_permisoPlan) as acciones, GROUP_CONCAT(a.descripcion ORDER BY p.id_permisoPlan) as descripciones
        FROM mfo_permisoplan p
        INNER JOIN mfo_accionsist a ON a.id_accionSist = p.id_accionSist 
        INNER JOIN mfo_plan t ON t.id_plan = p.id_plan 
        WHERE a.estado = 1
        AND t.tipo_plan = 1
        AND t.tipo_usuario = 2
        AND t.id_sucursal = 1
        GROUP BY t.id_plan
        ORDER BY p.id_permisoPlan;
